
To install core  pacckages,type the following in an R command window:


```R
if(!requireNamespace("BiocManager"))
    install.packages("BiocManager")

```

Install specific packages,e.g., "GenomicFeatures" and "AnnotationDbi", with


```R
BiocManager::install(c("GenomicFeatures", "AnnotationDbi"))
```

The install() fuction (in the BioManager packager) has arguments that change its default behavior;type ?install for further help.


Updata Installed Bioconductor Packages

Bioconductor packages, expecially those in the development branch, are updatad fairly regularly.To identify packages requiring updata within your version of Bioconductor, start a new session of R and enter


```R
BiocManager::install()
```
